and should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold')\n    dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n    # Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n    foreground_threshold_found = False\n    text_threshold_found = False\n\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n            foreground_threshold_found = True\n            assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n        elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n            text_threshold_found = True\n\n    # https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928\n\nWhen running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text brightness threshold setting\n(colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text) has no effect because the Chromium\nsetting name was renamed from 'TextBrightnessThreshold' to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'\nin Chromium 99 (Qt 6.4), but qutebrowser still uses the old name.\n\nThis test verifies that:\n1. Get the dark mode settings for Qt 6.4\n            versions = version.WebEngineVersions.from_pyqt('6.4.0')\n            darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=versions, special_flags=[])\n\n            # For Qt 6.4, the settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch\n            # and should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold')\n            dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n            # Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n            foreground_threshold_found = False\n            text_threshold_found = False\n\n            for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n                if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n                    foreground_threshold_found = True\n                    assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n                elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n                    text_threshold_found = True\n\n            # Get the dark mode settings for Qt 6.4\n        versions = version.WebEngineVersions.from_pyqt('6.4.0')\n        darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=versions, special_flags=[])\n\n        # For Qt 6.4, the settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch\n        # and should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold')\n        dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n        # Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n        foreground_threshold_found = False\n        text_threshold_found = False\n\n        for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n            if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n                foreground_threshold_found = True\n                assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n            elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n                text_threshold_found = True\n\n        # The bug: currently uses TextBrightnessThreshold instead of ForegroundBrightnessThreshold\n        assert foreground_threshold_found, (\n            \"Qt 6.4 should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' for the text threshold setting, \"\n            f\"but it was not found. Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n            foreground_threshold_found = False\n            text_threshold_found = False\n\n            for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n                if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n                    foreground_threshold_found = True\n                    assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n                elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n                    text_threshold_found = True\n\n            # However, qutebrowser's darkmode module only has three variants defined:\n\n1. **Variant.qt_515_2** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n2. **Variant.qt_515_3** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n3. **Variant.qt_63** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` (with new `IncreaseTextContrast` setting)\n\nWhen Qt 6.4 is detected, the version check at line 318 of darkmode.py returns `Variant.qt_63`:\n\n```python\nif versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):\n    return Variant.qt_63\n```\n\nThis causes Qt 6.4 to pass `TextBrightnessThreshold` to Chromium, which no longer recognizes this setting name. Chromium 6.4 expects `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`, so the setting is silently ignored.\n\n## Evidence\n\nLooking at the git history, commit `4e61bfedd` (\"Rename colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text\") shows that support for Qt 6.4 was planned:\n\n- Defines `Variant.qt_64`\n- Renames the config setting from `threshold.text` to `threshold.foreground`\n- Uses `copy_replace_setting()` method to change the Chromium key to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\n\nHowever, this commit also shows that the `copy_replace_setting()` method was planned but never implemented in the `_Definition` class.\n\nA later commit `2a10461ca` (\"Remove dark mode settings removed from Chromium\") attempted to remove the Qt 6.3 variant and make Qt 6.4 work, but this change does not appear in the current codebase.\n\n## Regression Test\n\nThe regression test at `/workspace/regression_test.py` demonstrates this bug:\n\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```\n\n**Test Results:**\n- `test_qt63_text_threshold_setting_name` - **PASSES** (Qt 6.3 uses correct `TextBrightnessThreshold`)\n- `test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name` - **FAILS** (Qt 6.4 incorrectly uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` instead of `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`)\n\n## Affected Code Sections\n\n### File: `/app/qutebrowser/browser/webengine/darkmode.py`\n\n**Lines 243-281**: Define variants and their settings\n- No Variant.qt_64 is defined\n- Variant.qt_63 uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n\n**Lines 279-281**: Qt 6.3 definition\n```python\n_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_515_3].copy_add_setting(\n    _Setting('increase_text_contrast', 'IncreaseTextContrast', _INT_BOOLS),\n)\n```\n\n**Lines 309-328**: Version detection\n```python\ndef _variant(versions: version.WebEngineVersions) -> Variant:\n    if versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):\n        return Variant.qt_63  # <- This causes Qt 6.4 to use Qt 6.3 definition\n    ...\n```\n\n## Chromium References\n\nAs per Chromium commit links found in the code:\n- Qt 5.14: Introduced `darkModeTextBrightnessThreshold`\n- Qt 5.15+: Renamed to `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n- Chromium 99.0 (Qt 6.4): Renamed to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\n  - See: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3344100\n\n## Config File\n\nThe configuration option is defined in `/app/qutebrowser/config/configdata.yml`:\n\n```yaml\ncolors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text:\n  default: 256\n  type:\n    name: Int\n    minval: 0\n    maxval: 256\n```\n\n## Impact\n\nUsers on Qt 6.4 cannot adjust the text brightness threshold for dark mode.
